margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Nitrogen pad not done as inhibitor is oxygen dependant.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Uses/ polystyrene, protective coatings, copolymer resins etc.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Odour threshold/ 0.15 ppm</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Surface tension / high\u201431.14 dynes/ cm at 19C</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Viscosity at 20C/ 1 mPas</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Solubility/ Negligible in water, soluble in alcohol and ether</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Does not react with water.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Floats on water</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Readily undergoes polymerisation when heated or exposed to light or an oxidising / peroxide catalyst. The polymerisation releases heat and may become explosive. Must be inhibited</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Prior loading tank / lines must be free of oxidising agents. Cleanliness to water white . If at all some shippers do wall wash it will be for suspended particles like zinc dust , rust and lint. Chlorides 10 ppm and colour 10 Apha.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Ensure the manifold sample is clear and bright prior loading.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">FOSFA/ Banned as any one of the last two cargoes in organically coated tanks (Epoxy ), and as the last cargo in stainless steel and inorganically coated tanks (Zinc )</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Ignited by heat and open flame. Fire or contamination may cause violent rupture of tank</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Avoid breathing vapours. Provide body and respiratory protection. Keep tanks cool with water spray.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Suspected carcinogen.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Vapour causes moderate irritation to the skin, liquid causes smarting of the skin and first degree burns on long exposure, inhalation or ingestion causes bodily harm. Styrene degreases the skin.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Irritates eyes and respiratory tract. Vapors cause weakness, dizziness, nausea and<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;sleepiness. Attacks the nervous system.STEL/ 10 000 ppm may be fatal in 30 to 60 minutes. Product can be absorbed through the skin, mucous,&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>membranes and eyes. Wear protective clothing</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Cargo not to be exposed to excessive heat. Alarm system to monitor cargo temperature should be provided</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Heating coils in tanks should be blanked.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Stowage adjacent to heated cargoes is not normally allowed. DOW allows maximum&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>adjacent cargo temperature 30</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Symbol; font-size: 13.5pt;\">\u00b0</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">C.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Styrene monomer creates humidity on the bulkheads of adjacent tanks, therefore in case of simultaneous loading of Styrene Monomer and Methanol in adjacent tanks, keep the level of Methanol always 2 \u2013 3 meters higher than level of Styrene Monomer to prevent water contamination of Methanol.&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Hot moist vapour condenses on cold surface.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Styrene is inhibited by 10- 15 ppm PTCB or tertiary butyl acetechol. Styrene can be stabilised by toluene too.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Vessel should be provided with \u201cInhibition Certificate\u201d from the manufacturer of cargo.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">&nbsp;The Certificate should specify:</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">The name and amount of additive present</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Whether the additive is oxygen-dependent</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Date additive was put in product and duration of effectiveness</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>Any temperature limitations qualifying the additive\u2019s effective lifetime</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>The actions to be taken should the length of voyage exceed the effective lifetime of the additive.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Styrene Monomer can form polymer residues and in case of epoxy coating&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>the trace quantity of styrene&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>will soak into&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>the paint film and only very slowly desorb.Odour and quality critical cargoes must not be carried for at least two voyages after the carriage of Styrene in epoxy tanks.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Has low electrical conductivity. Can generate electrical charges during high turbulence.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">To prevent polymerisation, present tank to surveyor as soon as practical .Never allow styrene to dry on the bulkheads.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Start washing with cold sea water one&nbsp;<span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span>machine circle and leave it until cleaning is started. Ensure lines are flushed .</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Empty the tank and start butterworthing with COLD sea water for 1 hour</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Then hot wash with 70C water for 1 hour.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Rinse with fresh water.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Steam for 2 hrs to eliminate odour</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Drain lines, mop up, dry</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">Use smell killer only is the tank is absolutely clean.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">If the next cargo is wall wash PTT will be a problem. Use inhibiter killer and recirculate. ( If your SS tank is NOT smooth, recirc with a emulsifier. )</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc9wb1sBFI/AAAAAAAAB5k/AXQZMGNt1-w/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc9wb1sBFI/AAAAAAAAB5k/AXQZMGNt1-w/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 13.5pt;\">-------CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )</span><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 13.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><u1:p></u1:p>  <br />\n<div style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">\u201c Open happiness \u201c \u2013 Coke cries gleefully.<br />\n<br />\n\u201c Good morning happiness\u201d \u2013 screams a swank cooking range advertisement.<br />\n<br />\nSurely marketing whizkid know zilch about happiness. It cant be bought or sold by money.<br />\n<br />\nHappiness is FREE. It is about filling up the space deep inside, or gratification of the soul. It is about equilibrium or dynamic balance between your SPIRIT , MIND AND MATTER. For life is a combination of spiritual, intellectual and physical aspects. It is achieved by deserving.<br />\n<br />\nHappiness has to overtake you. Say\u2014if you choose harmony over truth , you are overtaking happiness\u2014 it wont work.<br />\n<br />\nA cold fizzy coke will not make you happy. Never equate happiness with matter. It is more of spirit and mind. Inner peace, like peace at home will make you happy. A free swank cooking range could ignite the heart of a house wife , but it wont gratify her soul or cause her heart to sing.<br />\n<br />\nHappiness is a victory lap of positive forces over negative forces in your life. Now let us call the positive forces Pandavas, and the negative forces Kauravas. Just for the sake of simplicity. ( Pssst--both Ramayan and Mahabharata have been written backwards. The principle of nothing succeeds like success has been applied . If Ravan had won the war, we would have been shooting fire arrows at Ram on Dusshera day. Read both the epics and have an opinion for yourself )<br />\n<br />\nLet me make a list of Pandava forces, in a random order \u2013 for all prefer to have their priorities. Let us assume you have no needs which come from insufficiency, rather you have only wants . text-align: justify;\">\nWhat are you saying Ajit ji?! Those who only talk stats know shit about cricket! I am following cricket for 19 years day in &amp; day out. I have witnessed the action live &amp; not in a book or a newspaper or a website Greg Chapell was the one responsible for divide &amp; rule. He even went to Sachin during his coaching years and said that if we both get together then we can rule Indian Cricket but Sachin didn't support him in his endeavour. Ganguly is the one person that has revived Indian Cricket after the fixing scandals of 2000. He brought the best out of his players. I will give you instances, He got back retiring Javagal Shrinath back into Indian Team to play World Cup 2003. Also, Dravid was not supposed to be picked in that world cup but he fought with the selectors &amp; played him as a wicket keeper, that masterstroke revived Dravid's ODI Career. Ganguly was the one who picked the not so technical chote sheher ka ladka MS Dhoni &amp; backed him during his initial failures. He was the captain when India defeated the Invincible Aussies in Test Series in 2001. He was the captain when we went to the home ground of Aussies &amp; drew the Test Series 1-1 in a 4 match series. That was by far India's best performance ever and retained Border Gavaskar Trophy. The biggest contribution in winning the 2011 World Cup should be given to Ganguly. He backed Bhajji through out his captaincy. He made that Team! He was responsible for inclusion of young Yuvraj Singh in Champions Trophy of 2000. He was the one who backed the batting style of Sehwag &amp; kept him in the team for a long run.He was the one who backed Injury mein body Ashish Nehra. His contribution was immense in Test Careers of laxman &amp; kumble. Yes he has ego issues. I agree with that but who hasn't? If there was no ego then why would we have been here? 40+ average in those days 1996-2008 is really good. The pitches were not so flat like we had today &amp; the quality of bowlers was much better! He played Akram, Waqar, Shoaib,Walsh, Ambrose, Bond, Caddick,Gough, Donald, Vaas, McGrath, Warne, Murli, Vittori, Saqlain at their peak!I can go on &amp; on &amp; on.</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" id=\"bc_0_33BR\" style=\"margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replybox-single\" id=\"bc_0_33B_box\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; margin-top: 5px;\">\n</div>\n</li>\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_34B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"font-size: 16px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0.25em 0px 8px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n<img src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/zFdxGE77vvD2w5xHy6jkVuElKv-U9_9qLkRYK8OnbDeJPtjSZ82UPq5w6hJ-SA=s35\" style=\"border: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); max-width: 36px;\" /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c8374417057970977807\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_34M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/07328875349651029194\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">Drak</a></cite><span class=\"icon user\" style=\"font-weight: bold;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2018/03/sanatana-dharma-hinduism-exhumed-and.html?showComment=1520082480384#c8374417057970977807\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">March 3, 2018 at 6:38 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_34MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nAbhishek Sharma it's your word vs Captain's word !!<br />\n<br />\nAnd it's really presumptuous to think that Captain is speaking on the basis of stats alone! text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPtSGbzqaSI/AAAAAAAABcY/OcxBO63AGWQ/s1600/ethics.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPtSGbzqaSI/AAAAAAAABcY/OcxBO63AGWQ/s1600/ethics.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPtSJeAayzI/AAAAAAAABcc/ZnpvmqTuz4U/s1600/innovation.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPtSJeAayzI/AAAAAAAABcc/ZnpvmqTuz4U/s1600/innovation.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPtSLrCBuxI/AAAAAAAABcg/jjqzci15AIs/s1600/team.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPtSLrCBuxI/AAAAAAAABcg/jjqzci15AIs/s1600/team.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPtSOz3iNqI/AAAAAAAABck/sCpMkkQqSqM/s1600/compassion.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPtSOz3iNqI/AAAAAAAABck/sCpMkkQqSqM/s1600/compassion.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">ETHICS, INNOVATION, TEAM DYNAMICS, COMPASSION-- ideal core values.</span></div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><object width=\"320\" height=\"266\" class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://1.gvt0.com/vi/2UznXMCDH3k/0.jpg\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/2UznXMCDH3k&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/2UznXMCDH3k&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div><br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Play the video above while you read this post.</span></em><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">(Remember INTEGRITY is more than a core value --as it guarantees other values.)</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Our company values are like fingerprints, we leave them all over everything we do.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">As is inherent in our company symbol, our core values obviously are --</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">1) <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">High ethics.</span></div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Welcome to the high moral ground where committing a felony even to support the company is not a career move .</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We rely on own merit to push a case, not blatant use of personal charm as a way to wheel and deal. Our company has a conscience . Our clean reputation and absence of deception is our biggest intangible asset which is reflected in our brand equity and not on our balance sheet.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Our ethics are not abstract notions , but practical guides to employees on how to feel, act and behave. Ethical behavior is a habit in our company , not an act. All employees are part of the ethical fabric .</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We have a DEO ( designated ethics officer ) cum mentor to get this core value into the blood stream of the company , to oversee compliance , provide a frame work of conduct and to provide support to an employee who wants to do the right thing.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Our ethics champion is no lesser than the MD himself , with a moral barometer and an ethics radar to do ethical climate assessment. There exists a strong belief that it is acceptable to deliver bad news to the company or raise personal concerns.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Our mature ethics programmes have reduced voluminous codes of conduct to just a few sub core values like fairness, integrity, transparency, respect , tolerance for culture, responsibility , spirit of inclusion etc. Seminars are used to clarify ethics values , as sustaining an ethical culture is a continuous process without a finish line.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We trust our employees to do the right thing when confronted with a situation that provides no easy answers. We don\u2019t have yes-men who will not tell the truth to safeguard their jobs. We temper all technical judgments by the need to support and maintain human values.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We honour our contracts and don\u2019t cut corners. We do not allow conflicts of interest, which provide a competitive advantage to one client over another. We respect the intellectual property rights of our clients, and guard them zealously.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We do not advertise ourselves or our services in a deceptive manner, and will not misrepresent or allow the misrepresentation of the services by affiliates, associates, contractors, employees, partners and vendors.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We do not promote our own interest at the expense of the dignity of the marine profession. We obey the law in both letter and spirit. We maintain a safe and healthy working environment.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We do not encourage nepotism, fully aware that blood is a poor substitute for competence.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">##########</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">2) <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Innovation</span></div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">There is something about innovation that quickens our collective hearts. We recognize there is no such thing as instant innovation. The farmer must invest in the soil before he reaps a rich harvest. We nurture a climate where innovation happens.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Innovation at our neck of the woods is evolutionary not a revolutionary panic response to change . To innovate is not to reform, but to bring useful change. Changes need not be innovations but innovations are changes. Application of creativity is innovation.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We recognize that bureaucracy kills creativity. We encourage our people to use their imagination , listen to their their inner voice and use all their six senses to check assumptions and apply their creativity. We encourage creative dissent and we protect human feelings.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We brainstorm often to get feedback. We have a commitment not to allow our policies , procedures and rituals to get in the way of innovation. We can sense the drift of change and ensure that we are aligned to it in advance as surely as a ship enters a narrow channel. We take change by hand before it takes us by the throat. We give recognition to creative thinkers and innovative doers .</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We don\u2019t try to get our creative wild geese to fly in military formation. We recruit people who have the seeds of the future within them. Innovate or die\u2014is our slogan .</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Our organisational gatekeepers frame the environment that enables innovation, however innovation is enacted \u2013 recognised, developed, applied and adopted \u2013 through individual employees..</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">##########</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">3) <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Dynamics</span></div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We have reinvented team dynamics . Our team is a dynamic whole based on interdependence rather than on similarity or cloning. Our team acts in unity , almost like a single living organism, that requires to be nurtured to maintain its growth. We understand team chemistry\u2014the natural forces at play, to determine whether they are acting for ill or good and can make timely interventions to make the dynamics positive.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Our people are harmonious team players and there is a natural force of inclusion which results in transparent communications. They inspire the highest level of commitment from each other. Everyone is accountable to one another. They share similar values, attitudes, ideals and goals .</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Proper team dynamics ensures extraordinary results .Team dynamics consists of critical areas such as personal abilities, educational backgrounds, life experiences and personality compatibility of each exclusive teammate .</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Our HR department does TDP ( Team Dynamics Profiling ) to give us concrete indications on how the team will bond, interact and ultimately perform. Our seminars are basically team retreats where we enjoy our team rituals, chants and gleeful routines.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We encourage each person in the team to give both positive and negative feedback. We choose team players who will complement each other, rather than exclude each other, no matter what superstars they are.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">What we require is not well balanced individuals, rather individuals who balance well with each other . We devise strategies so that team players can feed off each other rather than cancelling out each other. Thus we remain united in our pursuit of our goals, resistant to disruptive forces.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Our inspirational team leadership uses emotional impact. We afford an inspirational environment to our high performance teams . Communications in our Company is a group process, and mutual trust and respect are maintained in order to keep the channels open. No body's perfect , but we believe that our team is.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Our team can produce a quality and quantity of work far higher than the sum of what the separate members could have ever produced on their own. Collective synergy of experience and expertise, accented with harmony, loyalty and camaraderie is indisputably our core asset.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">########</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">4) <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Compassion</span></div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We respect and appreciate culture in terms of itself. We are sensitive to cultural nuances . We listen and we respect local values . We think globally, but act locally. We understand that culture has a life of its own and is stronger than life and triumphs over death. We believe human beings have feelings unlike machines.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">Our human resources are not mere dehumanized code numbers or cheap labour to be exploited, thereby breeding indifference. They are our biggest assets. We recognize that people are not things and they need to be led and motivated rather than being managed.. When people do their jobs we get out of their way.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">We recognise that our employees are bread winners at home. Our company can grow only if our employees grow. We run a innovative organization which relies more upon shared ethos, than adherence to hard written rules. We have people feel and our HR dept knows how to monitor the pulse of our employees.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">If at all we criticize we do so in a constructive manner. We do not manipulate by unfair or insidious means. We assure the psychological, safety and social needs of our staff. No wonder our staff is eager to walk that extra mile to get things right\u2014 the XXXXX way.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">These core values represent our brand promise.</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">####################</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">COMMENTS:</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">I have worked for a lot of ignorant companies, who confuse goals with values. Their collective noses are stuck forever in a knothole. They get their knickers in a twist when they are reminded that --</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\"A goal is something you intend to accomplish. A value is something you believe in\"</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">It is better to keep away from such immature rubbish.<br />\n<br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc-6i0u0eI/AAAAAAAAB50/HLt-HDpS6pM/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc-6i0u0eI/AAAAAAAAB50/HLt-HDpS6pM/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )</div><div style=\"margin: 0px;\">..</div></div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "21", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/4931176710617495913/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "342652219409504448", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-12-05T12:14:00+05:30", "updated": "2010-12-26T09:46:44+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMjkzMzM3MDA0MzQ5Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/12/polymerisation-and-inhibition-on.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/342652219409504448", "title": "POLYMERISATION AND INHIBITION ON CHEMICAL TANKERS--  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPs0QTghfXI/AAAAAAAABYw/nX92q9Ub0SI/s1600/work+hard+play+hard+fcol.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"172\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPs0QTghfXI/AAAAAAAABYw/nX92q9Ub0SI/s320/work+hard+play+hard+fcol.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><br />\n</b></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">&nbsp;POLYMERISATION AND INHIBITION <o:p></o:p></b></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPs0reLEDDI/AAAAAAAABY0/Uf4DBXYqIWU/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPs0reLEDDI/AAAAAAAABY0/Uf4DBXYqIWU/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Polymerisation can happen by :--<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">An initiator ( reaction partner )<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Heat ( thermic polymerization )<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Light ( photo polymerization )<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Radiation ( radiation polymerization )<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Chemicals which polymerise form complex aggregates called polymers by the combination of two or more identical molecules from the original chemical which is a monomer.&nbsp; Monomers are among the purest organic chemicals produced.&nbsp; Inhibitors converted to free radicals halt a second reaction chain. Inhibitors react with reactive intermediates thus removing them from the reaction.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">When a single molecule reacts with another molecule of the same substance. A long chain molecule is formed having thousands of individual molecules. Can be with rapid evolution of heat to form sticky, resinous materials. Cargo then becomes viscous and unpumpable.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Some unsaturated unsaturated compounds with one or more double bondings are able to polymerise, like-- Vinyl compounds, Vinyliden compounds, Acryl compounds, Carbonyl compounds ( eg:aldehyde ), Styrene, Ethylene / propylene oxide, Ethylene, Propylene, Isobutylene, Butadiene, Isoprene.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Polymers are usually distinguished by a high molar mass (formula weight), often ranging into thousands or millions of grams per formula unit. Polymerization is a poly-reaction of a monomer compound whose molecule contains double bondings or rings . Ethylene is a highly flammable gaseous molecule with a formula weight (molar mass) of 32 grams per mol. When polymerized using a catalyst, it forms an insoluble solid called polyethylene. Polyethylene is a widely used commodity plastic. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Unstable chemicals decompose or polymerise. A decomposing chemical is stabilised and a polymerizing chemical is inhibited.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Chemicals like Acetone Cyanohydrin and Lacto Nitrile which decompose are stabilized by inorganic acid to prevent decomposition or poisonous gas will evolve.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Heat shortens life of the inhibitor. Inhibitors have a shelf life. &nbsp;Heat, light and radiation catalyses polymerization. Opposite of inhibitor is initiator. Add Sodium Naphtalene to Styrene and the tank gets polymerized.&nbsp; Hydrocarbons weaken inhibitors.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Inhibitors are not volatile. They are very difficult to remove by tank cleaning. PTT will be affected. An inhibitor killer can be used if next cargo is WWT.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">A test for inhibitor content of Styrene consists of mixing one part of Styrene is 3 parts of Methanol. If the mixture remains clear or slightly bluish the product is intact. A slightly white turbidity indicates polymerization or that the inhibitor is slightly consumed. If there is an unexplained temperature rise consult shippers and operators immediately. The action might be as drastic as jettisoning the parcel.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Polymerization reactions are exothermic reactions. Reaction speed is strongly influenced by catalysts ( usually metals ). Many polymerization reactions are started by heating and by liquids after the formation of Peroxides. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Inhibitors are added in very low concentrations\u201410 to 40 ppm. Unlike monomers inhibitors prefer to react with Oxygen, and this way the formation of Peroxides is prevented.&nbsp; Inhibitors have a shelf life and they have to be replenished.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">If the inhibitor is oxygen dependant NEVER nitrogen pad the tanks.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">The list of chemicals required to be inhibited is attached to this manual. &nbsp;Generally all monomers, Acrylates, and chemicals like Acetone Cyanohydrin, Benzyl Chloride, Butadiene, Iso Propyl Ether, Isoprene, Pentadiene, and Vinyl chemicals require to be inhibited.&nbsp; Ethylene oxide , Propelene oxide and Iso Butylene can also polymerise.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">No polymerising cargo can be loaded without a signed inhibitor certificate, a copy of which is attached to this manual.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">It must contain the following minimum information\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Name and amount of inhibitor<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Whether the additive is oxygen dependant<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Date inhibitor was added and length of its effectiveness<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Any temperature limitations qualifying the lifetime of the inhibitor<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Action to be taken in case the voyage length exceeds the effective life time of inhibitor<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Recommended method of determining additive level continued activity<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPs1uk2An1I/AAAAAAAABY4/WtwZSIsnNfc/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPs1uk2An1I/AAAAAAAABY4/WtwZSIsnNfc/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">You must remember that inhibitors added to liquid cargo may not inhibit reaction of cargo vapor in the ullage spaces. So it is imperative that after discharge of polymerizing cargoes , PV flame screens must be checked.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Polymerizing can take place if a Styrene Monomer tank is not cleaned for a few days.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Inhibitors are usually Amines, Phenols and Quinones. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Few examples are\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">TBC/ p-Tert Butyl Catecol---slightly soluble in water<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">HQ/ Hydroquinone---soluble in water<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">MEHQ/ Hydroquinone Mono Ethyl Ether----slightly soluble in water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">24M6BP/ 2.4 Dimethyl 6 Tert Butyl Phenol---insoluble in water<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Drying veg oils: even this is a sort of polymerization where molecules link together in a long chain making the oily residue more binding and tenacious.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Stabilizers prevent a compound from changing its chemical nature . <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">They\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">retard the chemical reaction<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">preserve chemical equilibrium<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">act as anti oxidants<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">keep pigments and other compounds in emulsion form<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">prevent colloids from precipitating<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Heat of Polymerisation\u2014The values is the heat liberated when the specified weight of the monomer polymerises to form the Polymer. In some cases the heat liberated is so huge that the tank can explode. The negative sign before the value indicates that heat is given off during the polymerization reaction.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Polymerization can be prevented by refrigeration or inhibition.. When temperature is too high the cargo will tend to evaporate. The initiator will be left behind. When the monomer condenses it can polymerise.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Ensure that extra inhibitor is supplied if the voyage is long from cold to warm climates. All cargo lines have to be drained and emptied back into tank. On warm days cool decks with sprinkler. Check cargo temperatures daily to ensure polymerization is not taking place.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"TxBrp4\" style=\"line-height: normal;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Immediately after dischg , and tank dry cert is obtained , cold SW wash and leave water inside the tank, including pipelines\u2014if terminal regulations permit.&nbsp; Ensure peep holes are cleaned properly. In case of polymerizing cargo fill cold water in common collector ASAP\u2014check interior with a torch\u2014clean out the drains physically. Water wash may be followed by warm ( Alkaline /<i> </i>Caustic solution).&nbsp; Water wash alone is insufficient to prevent PTT test failure .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">If the common collector is used for polymerizing cargoes\u2014open out the end covers and clean with water. Line blow to be done more than 4 times with polymerizing and solidifying cargoes.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"TxBrp3\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 10.2pt 94.95pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Washing polymerizing chemicals or frying Veg oils with hot water will result in polymerized layer&nbsp; which is very difficult to remove. Polymerization may also take place when a tank is not cleaned and left dirty for a few days. Since the added inhibitor is not volatile&nbsp; , condensation of the vapor will allow inhibitor free chemical to be formed. Cleaning of these cargoes should always start with a cold pre-wash as soon as possible after discharge, due to loss of inhibitor protection.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"TxBrp3\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 10.2pt 94.95pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">The relationship between VP of the inhibitor and VP of the cargo to be inhibited has a important &nbsp;bearing on the effectiveness of the inhibitor. If the VP of inhibitor is greater that that of the &nbsp;cargo then the vapours are protected. For this reason dual phase inhibitors are used for volatile cargoes\u2014one to protect the vapour space and the other to protect the liquid. Most inhibitors like &nbsp;Hydroquinone and Tertiary Butyl Catechol ( TBC ) are highly toxic .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"TxBrp3\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 10.2pt 94.95pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Many inhibitors are more soluble in water than the cargo- so water must be kept out\u2014or the &nbsp;concentration of the inhibitor will be reduced.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Certain cargoes do not have inhibitor \u2013so these cargoes must be carried under inert gas. In which case the Oxygen content must not exceed 0.2%</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"TxBrp3\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 10.2pt 94.95pt;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc_GDakjxI/AAAAAAAAB54/2Xie2SBOlnA/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc_GDakjxI/AAAAAAAAB54/2Xie2SBOlnA/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div style=\"background: #F8FCFF;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">-------CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 years in command )<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRbBk1dZoNI/AAAAAAAACZU/51tVlvDP8t8/s1600/IMG_0547.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"158\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRbBk1dZoNI/AAAAAAAACZU/51tVlvDP8t8/s320/IMG_0547.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "4", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/342652219409504448/comments"}}], "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/MjAxOS0wNC0yMlQxMTozNzoyOS43MjRa\""}
